<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology">Etymology</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Pronunciation_3">Pronunciation</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Dutch_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Dutch pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA nowrap">/sɛi̯n/</span></li>
<li><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r50165410" /><table class="audiotable" style="vertical-align: middle; display: inline-block; list-style: none; line-height: 1em; border-collapse: collapse; margin: 0;"><tbody><tr><td>sein (NL)<span class="ib-colon qualifier-colon">:</span></td><td class="audiofile"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><audio id="mwe_player_2" controls="" preload="none" data-mw-tmh="" class="mw-file-element" width="175" style="width:175px;" data-durationhint="2" data-mwtitle="nl-sein.ogg" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons"><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/30/Nl-sein.ogg" type="audio/ogg; codecs=&quot;vorbis&quot;" data-width="0" data-height="0" /><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/3/30/Nl-sein.ogg/Nl-sein.ogg.mp3" type="audio/mpeg" data-transcodekey="mp3" data-width="0" data-height="0" /></audio></span></span></td><td class="audiometa" style="font-size: 80%;">(<a href="/wiki/File:nl-sein.ogg" title="File:nl-sein.ogg">file</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table></li>
<li>Rhymes: <a href="/wiki/Rhymes:Dutch/%C9%9Bi%CC%AFn" title="Rhymes:Dutch/ɛi̯n"><span class="IPA nowrap">-ɛi̯n</span></a></li>
<li>Hyphenation: <span class="Latn" lang="nl">sein</span></li></ul>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Etymology 1"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=seigne&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="seigne (page does not exist)">seigne</a></i>, a northern variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/signe#Old_French" title="signe">signe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/signum#Latin" title="signum">signum</a></i>.<sup id="cite&#95;ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>1<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#doublet" title="Appendix:Glossary">Doublet</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/zegen#Dutch" title="zegen">zegen</a></i>.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Noun_3">Noun</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl">sein</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/seinen#Dutch" title="seinen">seinen</a></b>, <i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#diminutive" title="Appendix:Glossary">diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/seintje#Dutch" title="seintje">seintje</a></b>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)</span>
</p>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Estonian">Estonian</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Estonian"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_3">Etymology</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Finnic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Finnic language">Proto-Finnic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="urj-fin-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Finnic/saina" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Finnic/saina">&#42;saina</a></i>, borrowed from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Baltic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Baltic languages">Baltic</a></span> language, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv"><a href="/wiki/siena#Latvian" title="siena">siena</a></i>. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Finnish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Finnish language">Finnish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fi"><a href="/wiki/sein%C3%A4#Finnish" title="seinä">seinä</a></i> is of the same origin.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Pronunciation_4">Pronunciation</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>

</p>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_4">Etymology</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<ul class="etymonid" id="French:&#95;breast" data-lang="fr" data-id="breast"></ul><p><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#inherited" title="Appendix:Glossary">Inherited</a> from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Old_French:_old">sein</a></i>, from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/sinus#Latin:_curve" title="sinus">sinus</a></i>, from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Italic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Italic language">Proto-Italic</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="itc-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Italic/sinus&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Italic/sinus (page does not exist)">&#42;sinus</a></i>, from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/sinos&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/sinos (page does not exist)">&#42;sinos</a></i>. <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#doublet" title="Appendix:Glossary">Doublet</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/sinus#French" title="sinus">sinus</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href="/wiki/seno#Italian" title="seno">seno</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Romanian language">Romanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ro"><a href="/wiki/s%C3%A2n#Romanian" title="sân">sân</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romansh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Romansh language">Romansch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="rm"><a href="/wiki/sain#Romansch" title="sain">sain</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt"><a href="/wiki/seio#Portuguese" title="seio">seio</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href="/wiki/seno#Spanish" title="seno">seno</a></i>.

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Noun_7">Noun</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr">sein</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-fr p-form-of" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/seins#French" title="seins">seins</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/breast" title="breast">breast</a> (the chest)
<dl><dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">Sur votre jeune <b>sein</b> laissez rouler ma tête.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Let my head roll on your young <b>breast</b>.</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/breast" title="breast">breast</a>
<dl><dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">Elle a de gros <b>seins</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She has big breasts.</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#literary" title="Appendix:Glossary">literary</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> <a href="/wiki/womb" title="womb">womb</a>
<dl><dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">Elle a porté cet enfant dans son <b>sein</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She carried this child in her <b>womb</b>.</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/bosom" title="bosom">bosom</a>
<dl><dd><span class="h-usage-example collocation"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">au <b>sein</b> de la famille</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in the bosom of the family</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="h-usage-example collocation"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">le <b>sein</b> du Père</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the bosom of the Father</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Etymology 1"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#inherited" title="Appendix:Glossary">Inherited</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href="/wiki/sin#Middle_High_German" title="sin">sīn</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href="/wiki/sin#Old_High_German" title="sin">sīn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (suppleted with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/wesan%C4%85" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/wesaną">&#42;wesaną</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/beun%C4%85" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/beuną">&#42;beuną</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be, exist, become</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%81es-" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₁es-">&#42;h₁es-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be, exist</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/zijn#Dutch" title="zijn">zijn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href="/wiki/sien#Low_German" title="sien">sien</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. 
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Verb_2">Verb</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Verb"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de">sein</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#irregular" title="Appendix:Glossary">irregular</a></i>, <i>third-person singular present</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/ist#German" title="ist">ist</a></b>, <i>past tense</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/war#German" title="war">war</a></b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/gewesen#German" title="gewesen">gewesen</a></b>, <i>past subjunctive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/w%C3%A4re#German" title="wäre">wäre</a></b>, <i>auxiliary</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de"><strong class="selflink">sein</strong></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#copulative" title="Appendix:Glossary">copulative</a><span class="ib-comma label-comma">,</span>&#32;with a predicate adjective or predicate nominative</span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> to <a href="/wiki/be" title="be">be</a>
<dl><dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Das <b>ist</b> schön.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That <b>is</b> beautiful.</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Das <b>ist</b> ein Auto.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That <b>is</b> a car.</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#impersonal" title="Appendix:Glossary">impersonal</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> to <a href="/wiki/feel" title="feel">feel</a> <span class="mention-gloss-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss">to experience a condition</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren">)</span> <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r86744404">.mw-parser-output .object-usage-tag{font-style:italic}.mw-parser-output .deprecated{color:var(--wikt-palette-grey-lime-8,olivedrab)}</style>[<i>with</i> <span class="object-usage-tag"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dative_case" title="Appendix:Glossary">dative</a></span> <small>‘someone’</small> <i>and</i> <span class="object-usage-tag">adjective</span> <small>‘in some way’</small> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only for certain adjectives</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>]
<dl><dd><b>Usage:</b> In this sense <b>sein</b> is always conjugated in the third person singular and takes a dative noun. The impersonal subject <b>es</b> may be present, but is often taken as implied. For example: "<i>Mir <b>ist</b> warm,</i>" "<i>Mir <b>ist</b> es warm,</i>" and "<i>Es <b>ist</b> mir warm,</i>" may all be translated as "I'm warm," or literally as "(To) me (it) is warm." See Usage notes for the respective adjectives.</dd>
<dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><b>Ist</b> dir kalt&#63;</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Are you cold?</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Mir <b>ist</b> schlecht.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'm sick.</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Dem Mann <b>ist</b> schwindelig.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The man feels dizzy.</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Den Kindern <b>ist</b> langweilig.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The children are bored.</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#impersonal" title="Appendix:Glossary">impersonal</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> to <a href="/wiki/feel_like" title="feel like">feel like</a>, to be <a href="/wiki/in_the_mood" title="in the mood">in the mood</a> for <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r86744404" />[<i>with</i> <span class="object-usage-tag"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dative_case" title="Appendix:Glossary">dative</a></span> <small>‘someone’</small>, <i>along with</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/nach#German" title="nach">nach</a></b> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">+ <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dative_case" title="Appendix:Glossary">dative</a></span></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <small>‘something desired’</small> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/danach#German" title="danach">danach</a></b> <small>‘that thing’</small>, <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sometimes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <i>along with</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/zumute#German" title="zumute">zumute</a></b>]
<dl><dd><b>Usage:</b> As in the previous sense <b>sein</b> takes a dative noun and is always conjugated according to the impersonal subject <b>es</b>, although it is usually omitted.</dd>
<dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Uns <b>ist</b> nach einem Film zumute.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We feel like watching a movie.</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Mir <b>ist</b> nicht danach.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don't feel like it.</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#auxiliary" title="Appendix:Glossary">auxiliary</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> <span class="use-with-mention">forms the <a href="/wiki/present_perfect#English" title="present perfect">present perfect</a> and <a href="/wiki/past_perfect#English" title="past perfect">past perfect</a> tenses of certain intransitive verbs</span>
<dl><dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Er <b>ist</b> alt geworden.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>has</b> become old.</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> to <a href="/wiki/exist" title="exist">exist</a>; <a href="/wiki/there_be" title="there be">there to be</a>; to be <a href="/wiki/alive" title="alive">alive</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Was nicht <b>ist</b>, kann noch werden.</i> <span class="e-qualifier"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a common proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That which does not <b>exist</b> now, may come into existence.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Wenn ich nicht mehr <b>bin</b>, erbst du das Haus.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">When I <b>am</b> no more, you'll inherit the house.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a><span class="ib-comma label-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#colloquial" title="Appendix:Glossary">colloquial</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> to have the next <a href="/wiki/turn" title="turn">turn</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in a game, in a queue, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Du <b>bist</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It’s your turn.</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Du <b>bist</b> nach mir.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Your turn is after mine.</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a><span class="ib-comma label-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/childish" title="childish">childish</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> to <a href="/wiki/be" title="be">be</a> "<span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/it#English:_tag" title="it">it</a></span>"; to <a href="/wiki/be" title="be">be</a> the <a href="/wiki/tagger" title="tagger">tagger</a> in a game of <a href="/wiki/tag" title="tag">tag</a>
<dl><dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Du <b>bist</b>&#33;</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You'<b>re</b> <b>it</b>!</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Ich <b>bin</b> nicht mehr.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'<b>m</b> not <b>it</b> anymore.</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Alternative forms:
</p>
<ul><li><i>Past participle</i>: <span class="Latn" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/gewest#German" title="gewest">gewest</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete; poetical</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><i>Second-person plural preterite indicative</i>: <span class="Latn" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/waret#German" title="waret">waret</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">older; poetical</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<p>The subjunctive I (first and third person) and indicative (first person only) forms are also used as imperatives.
</p>
<ul><li><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><b>Seien</b> wir mal ehrlich.&#47;<b>Sind</b> wir mal ehrlich.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Let</b>’s <b>be</b> honest.</span></span></li>
<li><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><b>Seien</b> Sie mal ehrlich.</i> <span class="e-qualifier"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">second-person formal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Be</b> honest!</span></span></li></ul>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Etymology 2"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Middle_High_German">sein</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href="/wiki/sin#Middle_High_German" title="sin">sīn</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href="/wiki/sin#Old_High_German" title="sin">sīn</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/s%C4%ABn" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/sīn">&#42;sīn</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/s%C4%ABnaz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/sīnaz">&#42;sīnaz</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">his own, her own, its own, their own</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (a reflexive possessive), from genitive of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/sw%C3%A9" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/swé">&#42;swé</a></i> with denominative suffix <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/-n%C3%B3s" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/-nós">&#42;-nós</a></i>, equivalent to the genitive form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/se-" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/se-">&#42;se-</a></i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href="/wiki/sien#Low_German" title="sien">sien</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">his, its</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/zijn#Dutch" title="zijn">zijn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">his, its</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href="/wiki/sin#Danish" title="sin">sin</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">his, her, its, their</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/sin#Old_English" title="sin">sīn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">his, its</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Determiner">Determiner</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Determiner"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de">sein</strong></span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/his" title="his">his</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Daniel schickt <b>seiner</b> Schwester eine SMS.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Daniel is sending a text to <b>his</b> sister.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Der Kater spielt oft mit <b>seinen</b> Spielsachen.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The cat often plays with <b>his</b> toys.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/its" title="its">its</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">agreeing with a masculine or neuter noun</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">der Mond und <b>sein</b> Licht</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">the moon and <b>its</b> light</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">das Schaf und <b>seine</b> Lämmer</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">the sheep and <b>its</b> lambs</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#informal" title="Appendix:Glossary">informal</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used to express an approximate number, often with <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/so#German" title="so">so</a></i>.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Der kostet so <b>seine</b> zweihundert Euro.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That one costs around two hundred euros.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/one%27s" title="one&#39;s">one's</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Man muss <b>seinem</b> Herzen folgen.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">One must follow <b>one’s</b> heart.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading5"><h5 id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</h5><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Usage notes"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>When used as a pronoun, the nominative masculine takes the form <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/seiner#German" title="seiner">seiner</a></i>, and the nominative/accusative neuter takes the form <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/seines#German" title="seines">seines</a></i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/seins#German" title="seins">seins</a></i>.
</p>
<ul><li><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">mein Vater und <b>seiner</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">my father and his</span></span></li>
<li><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">mein Kind und <b>sein(e)s</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">my child and his</span></span></li></ul>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Pronoun">Pronoun</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Pronoun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de">sein</strong></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#archaic" title="Appendix:Glossary">archaic</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#genitive_case" title="Appendix:Glossary">genitive</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/er#German" title="er">er</a></i></span></span></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#archaic" title="Appendix:Glossary">archaic</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#genitive_case" title="Appendix:Glossary">genitive</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/es#German" title="es">es</a></i></span></span></li></ol>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Gothic">Gothic</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Gothic"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Romanization">Romanization</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Romanization"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="got">sein</strong></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">romanization of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Goth mention" lang="got"><a href="/wiki/%F0%90%8D%83%F0%90%8C%B4%F0%90%8C%B9%F0%90%8C%BD#Gothic" title="𐍃𐌴𐌹𐌽">𐍃𐌴𐌹𐌽</a></i></span></span></li></ol>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Hunsrik">Hunsrik</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Hunsrik"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_5">Etymology</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Middle_High_German">sein</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href="/wiki/sin#Middle_High_German" title="sin">sīn</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href="/wiki/sin#Old_High_German" title="sin">sīn</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/s%C4%ABn" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/sīn">&#42;sīn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">his</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#German">sein</a></i>.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Pronunciation_8">Pronunciation</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Hunsrik_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Hunsrik pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA nowrap">/ˈsaɪ̯n/</span></li>
<li>Rhymes: <a href="/w/index.php?title=Rhymes:Hunsrik/a%C9%AA%CC%AFn&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Rhymes:Hunsrik/aɪ̯n (page does not exist)"><span class="IPA nowrap">-aɪ̯n</span></a></li>
<li>Syllabification: <span class="Latn" lang="hrx">sein</span></li></ul>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Determiner_2">Determiner</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Determiner"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Indonesian">Indonesian</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Indonesian"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_6">Etymology</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Dutch">sein</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">signal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=seigne&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="seigne (page does not exist)">seigne</a></i>, a northern variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/signe#Old_French" title="signe">signe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/signum#Latin" title="signum">signum</a></i>. <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#doublet" title="Appendix:Glossary">Doublet</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="id"><a href="/wiki/sinyal#Indonesian" title="sinyal">sinyal</a></i>.
</p>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Pronunciation_10">Pronunciation</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=81" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Norwegian_Nynorsk_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Norwegian Nynorsk pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA nowrap">/sɛɪːn/</span> </li></ul>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Adjective_2">Adjective</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=82" title="Edit section: Adjective"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nn">sein</strong> (<i>neuter</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href="/wiki/seint#Norwegian_Nynorsk" title="seint">seint</a></b>, <i>definite singular and plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href="/wiki/seine#Norwegian_Nynorsk" title="seine">seine</a></b>, <i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href="/wiki/seinare#Norwegian_Nynorsk" title="seinare">seinare</a></b>, <i>indefinite superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href="/wiki/seinast#Norwegian_Nynorsk" title="seinast">seinast</a></b>, <i>definite superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href="/wiki/seinaste#Norwegian_Nynorsk" title="seinaste">seinaste</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/slow" title="slow">slow</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/late" title="late">late</a> (arriving after expected time)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/late" title="late">late</a> (near the end of a period of time)</li></ol>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_10">Etymology</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=92" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="West_Frisian">West Frisian</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=99" title="Edit section: West Frisian"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_12">Etymology</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=100" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Dutch">sein</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">signal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=seigne&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="seigne (page does not exist)">seigne</a></i>, a northern variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/signe#Old_French" title="signe">signe</a></i>.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Pronunciation_11">Pronunciation</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=101" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><span class="usage-label-accent"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Clay_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Clay Frisian">Clay</a></span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:West_Frisian_pronunciation" title="Appendix:West Frisian pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA nowrap">/sai̯n/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><span class="usage-label-accent"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wood_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Wood Frisian">Wood</a></span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:West_Frisian_pronunciation" title="Appendix:West Frisian pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA nowrap">/sɛi̯n/</span></li></ul>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Noun_12">Noun</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sein&amp;action=edit&amp;section=102" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fy">sein</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-fy p-form-of" lang="fy"><a href="/wiki/seinen#West_Frisian" title="seinen">seinen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-fy diminutive-form-of" lang="fy"><a href="/wiki/seintsje#West_Frisian" title="seintsje">seintsje</a></b>)</span>
</p>
